 halaat ye ban gaye ki kai telecom companiyon ko apana kaarobaar sametanaa padaa
 Now, after about three years, from September 5, Jio's broadband service 'jio Giga Fiber' is going to start
 sirf 700 rupee prati maheene kii shuruaati keemat kii is yojana main broadband ke alaava kai khaas sarvice di ja rahi he
 However, Reliance's entry into this segment may increase the difficulties for DTH and cable operators providing broadband services
 kya he Jio kii broadband sarvisariliance jeeyo ke broadband sarvice main nunatam 100 Mbps se 1 Gbps internet speed dene kii yojana he
 Apart from this, lifetime free phone calls, free HD TV and dish will be provided
 ye plan 700 rupee masik se shuru hokar 10,000 rupee masik tak honge
 Along with this, Jio has also offered unlimited international phone calls from the landline to the US and Canada at a monthly rental of Rs 500
 speed banegi chunautiriliance jeeyo ne broadband seva main nunatam 100 Mbps kii internet speed dene kaa elaan kiya he
 However this speed will be further increased to 1 Gbps
 telecom industry ke jaankaron kii maane to hai speed broadband sarvice kii vajah se market kii anya companiyon ke saamne ek nai chunauti khadi hogi
 Actually, in the cheapest plan of BSNL, users get 50mbps speed
 vahiin top-and plan main yugers ko 100mbps kii speed kaa ofer miltaa he
 Similarly, the speed of Airtel's V-fiber broadband service is 300mbps
 yahaan bataa den ki beete somvaar ko reliance industries ke chairman mukesh ambani ne anual general meeting ko sambodhit karte hue kaha, ‘‘bharat main jeeyo giga fibre kii sabase nunatam speed 100 embipies hogi
 We have plans to provide speeds up to 1 Gbps under this
 ’’isi tarah 2020 ke madhya tak jeeyo giga fibre ke premium graahak ghar baithe film ke relies ke din hi use dekh sakenge
 Jio has named it 'first Day First Show'
 iskaa bada nuksaan multiplex ko uthaanaa pad saktaa he
 Narrowband Internet of Things: Reliance Jio plans to connect at least one billion devices on its Narrowband Internet of Things (nbiot) platform
 isse company ko lagbhag 20,000 karod rupee salanaa aamadani ho sakati he
 With its use, data generated from billions of smart sensors across the country will be collected reliably at the lowest cost
 ambani ne kaha, 'jeeyo kaa iot plateform 1 janvari 2020 se vyavsaayik upyog ke liye uplabdh ho jayega
 However, in this segment, Jio is expected to face other companies such as Tata Communications, Bharti Airtel and Vodafone Idea

 People also know this date as Akshaya Tritiya
 lekin yah tithi ek or myne main behad khaas he
 On this day Lord Parashurama, the sixth incarnation of Lord Vishnu, was also born
 bhagwaan parashuram rishi jamadagni or renuka ke putr the
 Parashurama is considered the god of justice
 vah apane mata-pita ke aagyaakaari putr the
 Despite this, he had cut his mother's neck
 aaie jaanate hai aakhir kyon parashuram ji ko apni maa kii gardan kaatani padi or phir kya hua unke saath
 According to the Brahmavarivata Purana, Srihari was the fourth child of Lord Parshuram Mata Renuka, the eighth incarnation of Vishnu, and Rishi Jamadagni
 shastr vidya or shastron ke gyaata bhagwaan parashuram ko ek baar unke pita ne ajna di ki wo apni maa kaa vadh kar de
 Lord Parashuram was a very obedient son
 unhone apane pita kaa aadesh pate hi turant apane parashu se apni maa kaa sir unke dhad se alag kar diya
 Seeing his orders, Lord Parashuram's father Rishi Jamadagni was very pleased with his son
 pita ko prasann dekh parashuram ne apane pita se maa renuka ko punah jivit karne kaa aagrah kiya
 Jyotishacharya Pandit Arunesh Kumar Sharmane told that Parashurama is considered to be the charge of Lord Vishnu
 unhone parashuram dwaara mata renuka vadh kii katha ko vistaar se bataate hue kaha ki ekbar rishi patni sarovar main snaan ke liye gai hui thi
 Incidentally, King Chitraratha was boating there
 raja ko dekh rishipatni ke hriday main vikaar utpann ho gaya or vah vahaan se usee manodasha main ashram laut ain
 When sage Jamadagni saw this distorted condition of his wife in the ashram, he came to know everything
 jisaki vajah se rishi behad krodhit ho gaye
 He first ordered the slaughter of mother to Parashurama's elders
 lekin maa se mohavash unke kisi bhi putr ne unki is ajna kaa paalan nahin kiya
 But when the father asked Parashurama to slay the mother, he obeyed the father's orders literally
 is par rishi ne ajna na maanane vaale putron ko vivek vichaar kho dene kaa shraap diya
 Pleased with Parashurama, he asked him to ask for the groom he wanted
 is par parashuram ne apane pita se mata ko punahjivit karne kaa vardaan mangakar apni maa ko navajivan pradaan kiya
 Seeing the sharp intellect of his son, the overjoyed Rishipita blessed Parashurama to earn fame till Dikdiganta and to be a master of all scriptures and weapons
 lekin parashuram ji ne pita ke kehane par apni maa kaa vadh kiya tha
 Due to which he also felt the sin of maternal murder
 unhen apane is paap se mukti bhagwaan shiv kii kathor tapasya karne ke baad mili
 Lord Shiva bestowed Parashurama with the Parashu weapon for the welfare of the dead, which is why he was later called Parashurama

 is trailor main sabase khaas baat he ki spide-main kaa kirdaar nibhaane vaale tom holand (tom Holland) ne trailor ke shuruyaat main disclemur ke taur par khud aate hai or bataate hai yadi aapane abhi tak 'avengers andgem' (avengers Endgame) nahin dekha he to is trailor ko abhi na dekhen, varanaa yah spiler kaa kaam karegi

 spidar-main: for from home (spider-man: Far From Home) kaa trailor kaaphi damdaar he

 kehete hai ki itihaas apane aap ko jarur doharaata he
 The wheel of time definitely turns
 2 saansadon vaali bhartiya janata party aaj 300 se zyada saansadon ke saath satta ke shikhar par he
 Its strength is that once again at the top of power, something has been seen that was seen even two decades ago
 desh kaa pradhanmantri uttar pradesh se or desh kaa grih mantri gujarat se
 What the bjp-vajpayee-advani duo did, is now repeated by the modi-shah duo
 
 
 
 When Vajpayee and Advani became PM-HM when the Bharatiya Janata Party came to power under the leadership of Atal Bihari Vajpayee, there were discussions between him and LK Advani
 donon ne bhaajapa ko farsh se arsh par le jane kaa kaam kiya
 In 1998, when Atal Bihari Vajpayee, who was elected from Lucknow in Uttar Pradesh, became the Prime Minister of the country, LK Advani remained second in that government
 adwani gujarat ke gandhinagar se saansad chune gaye, pehle vah grahamantri bane or baad main up pradhanmantri
 modi-shah reiterated history: Now after nearly two decades, history has taken a turn once again
 bhartiya janata party lagaataar duusari baar purna bahumat ke saath satta main he, narendra modi phir ek baar pradhanmantri hai
 The parliamentary constituency of PM is Varanasi in Uttar Pradesh
 apane duusare kaarykaal main narendra modi ne apane sabase khaas amit shah ko grih mantri banaaya
 Those who have come from Gujarat's Gandhinagar seat
 aise main centre main ek baar phir vahi PM-HM kaa formula apanaaya gaya he, jo vaajapeyi-adwani ke samay main doharaaya gaya tha
 Significantly, this time LK Advani, called the Iron Man of the Bharatiya Janata Party, did not get the ticket
 1991 se vah gandhinagar se hi saansad ban rahe the, unki jagah is baar amit shah ne lee
 As party president he contested from there and won by record votes
 khaas baat ye bhi he ki isse pehle narendra modi jab gujarat ke mukhyamantri the, to bhi unhone apane jodidar amit shah ko rajya kaa grahamantri banaaya tha
 As Union Home Minister Amit Shah is responsible, this time there are many issues which are always in discussion in the country
 phir chaahe vah jammu-kashmir se judaa dhara 370, anuchhed 35A kaa masalaa ho yaa phir purvottar main lagu kiya ja rahaa NRC kaa mudda
 In the previous term of the Modi government, there was a lot of controversy on these issues
 agar aapkaa koi bank acount nahin he to pareshaan mat hoie
 In a few days every citizen of India will have their own bank account
 darasal, rigerv bank of india ke ek ne panel suzav diya he ki 2016 tak desh ke har aadmi ke paas bank acount ho or iske liye khaas tarah ke bank khole jaaen jahaan kam aay varg ke log bhi paise jamaa kar sake
 The panel of RBI suggests that the bank should have facilities for withdrawing, paying and depositing the money at least 15 minutes away from the customer's home
 panel ke pramukh nachiket mor ne kaha he ki 01 janvari 2016 tak har naagarik jisaki umr 18 saal kii ho, uske paas apana pul sarvice, surakshit or electronic acount hona chahie
